[30;1m74 | [0m[35mSay we have two components that share a set of credentials. We don't want to[0m
[30;1m75 | [0m[35mhave to specify the same set of credentials twice, so instead, we use alternate[0m
[30;1m76 | [0m[35mkeys which let you specify other keys to look at for a configuration value.[0m
[30;1m77 | [0m[35mThis lets us have both components look at the same keys for their credentials[0m
[30;1m78 | [0m[35mand then we only have to define them once.[0m
